<L.6.1>
<Z>Updates and Dead Hardware <C> It's been an eventful week or so. For some time I've known I had to rewrite www.pbmsports.com because <L.31.1>
it was originally authored with Frontpage 2000 (older than legacy) and Windows 11 won't touch it. So I started on that Friday morning<L.31.1>
last week, and a few hours later my legacy Windows PC (which was stuck on Windows 10) suddenly died, and with it access to Frontpage. <L.31.1>
Pretty lucky timing, and all of that follows on my Zip Drive (used to transfer orders and results from the legacy machine I run games <L.31.1>
on to my Windows PC which actually talks to the internet) also dying (I have a now sourced a new one). As far as www.pbmsports.com, <L.31.1>
you'll see that the "Latest News" has moved (at present to a Test URL and over the next few weeks I'll rewrite the website with <L.31.1>
the information and news which is relevant to 2025 rather than 1995 - when it was maybe state of the art). Welcome to 2025....<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Deadlines <C> On a more general note, I am pondering whether to move deadlines around in the New Year. I moved games to Saturday<L.31.1>
way back when because I was working (and commuting) midweek, but now I'm not I've the option of running them on a weekday, which may<L.31.1>
be more family friendly so I don't lose my time over the weekend. Please keep an eye on messages, as I may move turns to a weekday<L.31.1>
(it'd probably be a Friday or a Monday). I'll pick this up in the New Year......<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Processing and Late Turns <C> Please note that the deadline is 9am Saturday, UK time, but appreciate I may run games Saturday or<L.31.1>
Sunday, and don't chase me up for "missing turns" until Monday. If I've got an issue which means turns delayed beyond that, you <L.31.1>
should find an update on www.pbmsports.com in the Latest News section, so please check there first.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Online Turnsheets <C> Please make sure when you input turns online you get the week/turn number correct (it's on your turnsheet).<L.31.1>
If you get it wrong, there's a risk the turn gets missed. Please also avoid double submission of turns - if they're within minutes<L.31.1>
the system will only take the latest set, but if they're spread out both may be input and you'll get charged 0.1 credit.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Slack <C> There's an independent (i.e. I'm not on it) group on Slack of various players in various games (Gameplan, Raceplan, <L.31.1>
Baseball, etc) covering things run here (and probably offering hints and advice, which may or may not be accurate). For more<L.31.1>
information, go to gameplanpbm.slack.com, or for an invite contact Alan Milnes on alan@gameplan.org.uk<L.31.1>
